Func DAOBUOCTRONGMAY()
	If Not $g_bComboSent Then
		_SendComboOnce()
	EndIf
	GUICtrlSetData($CRACK, "10")
_DAOBUOCTRONGMAY()  ;Checkpoint 1609
	Local $start = TimerInit()
	While TimerDiff($start) < 1
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "3226673381")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET2, "1078633983")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET3, "1072210765")
	WEnd

_DAOBUOCTRONGMAY()  ;Checkpoint 1610
